Decklists: Place 9 to 90
========================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 15, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff










Below you can find all the rest of the Day 2 decklists, all 82 of them, ordered by round 15 standings. Happy Valentine's Day from your friendly text coverage staff who spent the evening of that typing up decklists. (No really, we're fine!)
